        <p style="text-align: left;">
          In this document you will find all the release notes pertaining MediaSpace
        </p>
        
        <p style="text-align: left;">
          If this is your first time working with KMS, it is highly recommended that you take time to view the <a href="http://videos.kaltura.com/category/4_Tutorials%3E1_MediaSpace+Overview/10731711" target="_blank">Kaltura MediaSpace Overview Videos</a> also.
        </p>
        
        <p style="text-align: left;">
          If you are unable to find the information that you are looking for here, please use the search bar above to search for the information you seek, or report a missing information: "<a href="http://knowledge.kaltura.com/node/86">Couldn't find what you were looking for</a>?” form.
        </p>
      </td>
    </tr>

</table>

<span style="color: #484848; font-size: 18pt; font-weight: bold;"><a name="v5_52"></a>Version 5.52.10</span>

These release notes pertain to Kaltura MediaSpace 5.52.10, released on October 10, 2016. 

<p class="mce-heading-3">
  What's New in This Release
</p>

*   **Add Collaborators during upload** -  KMS admins can allow adding co-editors and co-publishers during upload of an entry in KMS or KAF. This can be configured in *UploadFormEnabled *field in the *mediaCollaboration *module.
*   **Default 'End Time' of Publishing Schedule** -The default has been changed to 'no end time'.
*   **'KMS GO' iOS App** - MediaSpace iOS Mobile Application is now available on the Apple store. You can read more [here][1].

 [1]: https://knowledge.kaltura.com/mediaspace-ios-mobile-application-v201-release-notes

<span style="color: #484848; font-size: 18pt; font-weight: bold;"><a name="v5_51"></a></span><span style="color: #484848; font-size: 18pt; font-weight: bold;">Version 5.51.12</span>

These release notes pertain to Kaltura MediaSpace 5.51.12, expected to be released on September 12, 2016. 

<p class="mce-heading-3">
  What's New in This Release
</p>

*   **oEmbed Change** -  The oEmbed Endpoint in KMS is now able to accept the entry page URL as input and not only the copied link from the 'share / oEmbed' tab. In addition to this type of URL: *https://[MediaSpace  URL]/id/[entry ID]?width=400&height=285&playerId=12345678*  this type of URL may be used: *https://[MediaSpace URL]/media/[Entry Name]/[Entry ID].* This improves the flexability with oEmbed-supported destinations. You can read more [here][2].

 [2]: https://knowledge.kaltura.com/mediaspace-oembed-integration

<p class="mce-heading-2">
  <a name="v5_49"></a>Version 5.49.07
</p>

These release notes pertain to Kaltura MediaSpace 5.49.07, released July 18, 2016. 

<p class="mce-heading-3">
  What's New in This Release
</p>

*   **Channel Playlist Page ** – **new look option. **A new option for the channel playlist page is now available to choose from. A KMS admin can configure that new look playlistPluginType field in playlistPage module. Use ‘On Page’ to display a unique playlist page look for the application (the way it was presented so far) . Use ‘In Player’ to display the new option for the channel playlist, using the default player's studio look in the page.

<a name="kms5_47" style="color: #484848; font-size: 18pt; font-weight: bold; background-color: #ffffff;"></a><span style="color: #484848; font-size: 18pt; font-weight: bold;">Version 5.47.04</span>

These release notes pertain to Kaltura MediaSpace 5.47.04, released June 19, 2016. 

<p class="mce-heading-3">
  What's New in This Release
</p>

*   **Persistent Cookies** - On top of the existing session time configuration, KMS now supports persistent cookies to maintain the user login-state. The KMS administrator has 2 options to choose from for the user login state:

1.  A specific session length for the user (in auth/sessionLifetime)
2.  A persistent cookie which gives users endless session time (until cookies are deleted)

<p style="padding-left: 60px;">
  Notes: Option #2 is implemented as a custom KMS module.  To enable this optioin on a KMS instance, please submit a request to Kaltura support or your Kaltura representative. Persistent cookies might raise security concerns as they hold an open session until cookies are deleted. Option #1 is no longer dependent on the KMS SaaS production update. (Sessions are ended no matter what the length was.) From now on, the session length is the only parameter for the login-state.
</p>

*   **Slides on Remote Storage** - In accounts that are set with remote storage configuration, slides on entries are now stored and played from the remote storage location.
*   **Korean** – Korean was added to the Languages list.
*   **UI Changes**
*    The following lists the text changes in the Publishing Schedule actions in the edit entry/details and in the upload form:
*   "scheduling" changed to "publishing schedule”
*   "any time" changed to "always"
*   "specific range" changed to "specific time frame"
*   Explanation text was added “(The time range in which this media will be visible to users in published channels/categories.)”

*   The animated GIF in the “Import Channel” action was replaced.

<p class="mce-heading-2">
  <span style="font-size: 18pt;"><a name="kms5-45"></a>Version 5.45.01</span>
</p>

These release notes pertain to Kaltura MediaSpace 5.45.01, released June 6, 2016. 

<p class="mce-heading-3">
  What's New in This Release
</p>

*   **Analytics for co-editors** - Co-editors can now see analytics page for the media they co-edit

<p class="mce-heading-3">

<p class="mce-heading-2">
  <a name="KMS5_44"></a>Version 5.44.03
</p>

These release notes pertain to Kaltura MediaSpace 5.44.03, released May 23, 2016. 

<p class="mce-heading-3">
  What's New in This Release
</p>

*   **Scheduled Publishing Improvements** – including the following:

1.  Schedule input from KMC is visible in KMS.
2.  It is possible to input a start date without an end date. Select the Clear’ option from the data drop down menu.
3.  It is possible to select start or end dates that are prior to the current date.
4.  Publish schedule timezone presentation - Entries where Scheduling was set outside of KMS (thus time zone is not specified on the Entry) will show Scheduling in the user's local time zone, per current Scheduling functionality. Entries where Scheduling was set in KMS (thus time zone is specified on the Entry) will show Scheduling in the timezone specified by the KMS user who set the Scheduling

<p class="mce-heading-2">
  <a name="KMS_5_43"></a>Version 5.43.07
</p>

These release notes pertain to Kaltura MediaSpace 5.43.07, released May 10, 2016. 

<p class="mce-heading-3">
  What's New in This Release
</p>

*   **Upload Slide Deck** - MediaSpace users can now upload a full deck of slides to present alongside their media (dual-screen experience), using the timeline functionality. Prior to this addition, users could only add one slide at a time. Any user will be able to upload a PPT, PPTX or PDF file and the slides their will automatically create slides within the video. Admins can enable this in *Chapters* module with the *enableFullDeck* field. For more information read [here][3].

 [3]: https://knowledge.kaltura.com/kaltura-player-editingdeleting-chapters-and-slides

<a name="KMS5_41" style="color: #484848; font-size: 18pt; font-weight: bold; background-color: #ffffff;"></a><span style="color: #484848; font-size: 18pt; font-weight: bold;">Version 5.41.07</span>

These release notes pertain to Kaltura MediaSpace 5.41.07, released April 10, 2016. 

<p class="mce-heading-3">
  What's New in This Release
</p>

*   **Dynamic chunk size upload** - In order to improve upload performance, KMS now dynamically changes the uploaded chunk size. The upload starts with a minimum-size of chunk, (1MB) then makes intelligent decision for what should be the next chunk size based on upload capabilities, and so on (max chunk size of 50MB)
*   **Analytics for Youtube entries **- videos that are originated in youtube (presented and linked to KMS through the youtube module) now include the analytics pages, similar to other entry types. Note: analytics for these entries include metrics for engagement inside KMS only and not aggregated with youtube playback analytics.

<a name="v5_40_11" style="color: #484848; font-size: 18pt; font-weight: bold; background-color: #ffffff;"></a><span style="color: #484848; font-size: 18pt; font-weight: bold;">Version 5.40.11</span>

These release notes pertain to Kaltura MediaSpace 5.40.11, released February 14, 2016. 

 

<p class="mce-heading-3">
  What's New in This Release
</p>

*   **Interactive Video Quiz**<span style="font-weight: bold;"> - </span>the ability to create, playback and report quizzes and surveys inside video content. For more written details read <a href="http://knowledge.kaltura.com/node/1677" style="font-weight: bold;">here</a> and for short video tutorials see <a href="http://videos.kaltura.com/category/4_Tutorials%3EInteractive+Video+Quiz/40511741" style="font-weight: bold;">here</a>.
*   <span style="font-weight: bold;"></span>**New Channel Details View** – An option for a new channel page table view was added to the admin console.
*   **Entry List ****UI Change** - The user name was moved to the bottom of the details, instead of its current location below the title.
*   **Channel Playlist UI Changes** – In the Channel edit page, in the Playlist tab, the 'Save' and 'Cancel' buttons were removed.  The channel playlists order is now saved automatically. In addition, the search was moved to the right side of the page.

<a name="v5_38_06" style="color: #484848; font-size: 18pt; font-weight: bold; background-color: #ffffff;"></a><span style="color: #484848; font-size: 18pt; font-weight: bold;">Version 5.38.06</span>

These release notes pertain to Kaltura MediaSpace 5.38.06, released January 17, 2016.

<span style="color: #828a8c; font-size: 14pt; font-weight: bold;">What's New in This Release</span>

*   **CaptureSpace Lite** - New MediaSpace instances will not include Kaltura Screen Recorder (KSR) and will only receive CaptureSpace Lite. To learn more about CaptureSpace Lite, read the <a href="http://knowledge.kaltura.com/node/1300" target="_blank">admin guide</a>, the <a href="http://knowledge.kaltura.com/node/1631" target="_blank">user guide</a> or watch [video tutorials][6].
*   **UI changes**
*   The text on the “Add Media” button in a channel or category (for cases where you want to add content to a channel or category) was changed to “Add to Channel” or “Add to Gallery” respectively.
*   The location of “Add New” button in channel or category (in case you want to create new content to be added) was changed – lowered 1 line.

*   **Default player version of ‘Embed Playlist’ in Channel Playlist** - version was updated to 2.38.3.

 [6]: http://videos.kaltura.com/category/4_Tutorials%3EKaltura+CaptureSpace+Lite/38629551?mkt_tok=3RkMMJWWfF9wsRovuarAZKXonjHpfsX57uUrXq%2B%2Bhokz2EFye%2BLIHETpodcMT8FgMK%2BTFAwTG5toziV8R7nNKM1z3tgQUxTr

<p class="mce-heading-3">
  <span style="color: #484848; font-size: 24px;"><a name="v5_37_06"></a>Version 5.37.06</span>
</p>

These release notes pertain to Kaltura MediaSpace 5.37.06, released January 3, 2016.

<span style="color: #828a8c; font-size: 14pt; font-weight: bold;">What's New in This Release</span>

*   **Catalan Support - **MediaSpace was localized to Catalan. The Admin can change MediaSpace instance language in *Application/Language/ca-es*
*   **Table view for My Media -** A table view was added to the existing Collapsed/Detailed views in My Media. The Admin can change it in *Gallery/tableView*
*   **PHP 5.6 support** - MediaSpace now supports PHP 5.6.

<a name="v5_35" style="color: #484848; font-size: 18pt; font-weight: bold; background-color: #ffffff;"></a><span style="color: #484848; font-size: 18pt; font-weight: bold;">Version 5.35.09</span>

These release notes pertain to Kaltura MediaSpace 5.35.09, released December 06, 2015.

<span style="color: #828a8c; font-size: 14pt; font-weight: bold;">What's New in This Release</span>

*   **Media Scheduling - **Users can now create content and set its publishing start time and end time. KMS admin can set this feature by enabling *Scheduling* module in the KMS admin console. For more information read [here][7].
*   **Upload Speed improvement - **Chunks size in KMS upload were increased from 1MB to 10BM which reduces upload time.

 [7]: http://knowledge.kaltura.com/scheduling

<a name="v5_33" style="color: #484848; font-size: 18pt; font-weight: bold; background-color: #ffffff;"></a><span style="color: #484848; font-size: 18pt; font-weight: bold;">Version 5.33.03</span>

These release notes pertain to Kaltura MediaSpace 5.33.03, released November 9, 2015.

<span style="color: #828a8c; font-size: 14pt; font-weight: bold;">What's New in This Release</span>

*   **Import Content into a Channel - **Channel managers can import content into their channel from any other channel they manage. KMS Admin can enable this for all channel managers in the new *Importchannel *module. See <a href="http://knowledge.kaltura.com/node/1557" target="_blank">Import Channels Feature Description</a> for more information.
*   **Additional actions on Groups in Channels and Categories - **Additional actions have been added for Category and Channel Managers to improve managing groups in their categories or channels.  Auto-completion of a group's name is available when adding a group, as well as the capability of deleting a group from the category/channel. These actions may be enabled through the KMS admin using the fields '*findGroupUserSuggestions*' and '*enableGroupActionMenu*' in the  '*Channelmembers*' and 'C*ategorymembers*' modules.

<p class="mce-heading-2">
  <a name="V5_27_05"></a><span><a name="v5_30_05"></a>Version 5.30.05</span>
</p>

These release notes pertain to Kaltura MediaSpace 5.30.05, released September 21, 2015.

<p class="mce-heading-3">
  What's New in This Release
</p>

*   **Changes in Browser Support for KSR - **The note in the Kaltura Screen Recorder for Chrome users has been changed. The new version of the Chrome browser and Microsoft’s recent release of the Edge browser do not support Java plugins. Due to this recent change, te Kaltura Screen Recorder (KSR) is no longer supported in the following browsers due to the Java dependency:
*   Google Chrome; Version 45 & up
*   Microsoft Edge; All Versions

To use Kaltura Screen Recorder (until a solution for Chrome and Edge support is found), please use another browser such as Safari, Internet Explorer, or Firefox.

The note in KSR reflects this information.

<p class="mce-heading-2">
  <a name="V5_27_05"></a><span style="font-size: 18pt;">Version 5.28.06</span>
</p>

These release notes pertain to Kaltura MediaSpace 5.28.06, released August 24, 2015.

<p class="mce-heading-3">
  What's New in This Release
</p>

*   **First Loaded Tab - **You can now select which tab will be loaded first in the Categories page. The options are: Media, Category Moderation or Channel Categories.   Enable this feature through the firstTabLoad field in the KMS Admin Console > Gallery module.
*   **Replace Media from URL - **The Replace Video tab now includes the option to replace media from a URL. Enable this feature through the replaceMediaFromUrl field in the KMS Admin Console > Replacemedia module.

<p class="mce-heading-3">
  <a name="v5_22_06"></a>Version 5.22.07
</p>

These release notes pertain to Kaltura MediaSpace 5.22.07, released May 4, 2015.

 <a name="V_5_9_04" style="color: #828a8c; font-size: 14pt; font-weight: bold; background-color: #ffffff;"></a><span style="color: #828a8c; font-size: 14pt; font-weight: bold;">What's New in this Release</span>

*   **Refresh My Media **– The Refresh option was added to the My Media window to provides a view of the recently added entries to My Media. Due to caching constraints, an entry may appear in the search results for example, but may not not appear in the My Media page. The Refresh option overcomes this constraint and displays the most recently added entries. To access the Refresh option, in the My Media window, select Refresh from the Actions drop down menu.  
      
    
*   **A note was added in the Kaltura Screen Recorder for Chrome users** - As of the latest version of Chrome (42), released last week, Google has decided to block Java by default, as described <a href="https://java.com/en/download/faq/chrome.xml" target="_blank">here</a>. The Kaltura Screen Recorder (KSR) will not function in instances of Chrome that have recently been installed or which have auto-updated to the latest version. The Kaltura Screen Recorder continues to function properly in all other major browsers. To ensure that the Kaltura Screen Recorder continues to work properly in Chrome (42), Chrome needs to be set to use Java, using this flag: <chrome://flags/#enable-npapi>. For more information read <a href="http://knowledge.kaltura.com/troubleshooting-kaltura-screen-recorder#screen+recorder" target="_blank">here</a>. If a user is using the Chrome browser, version 42, and did not enable the NPAPI flag, a message will be displayed in the KSR screen.

        <strong>Summary</strong>
      </td>
    </tr>
  </thead>
  
  <tbody>
    <tr>
      <td>

          KMS-6620
        </p>
      </td>

<p class="mce-heading-3">
  Version 5.21.06
</p>

These release notes pertain to Kaltura MediaSpace 5.21.06, released April 26, 2015.

<a name="V_5_9_04" style="color: #828a8c; font-size: 14pt; font-weight: bold; background-color: #ffffff;"></a><span style="color: #828a8c; font-size: 14pt; font-weight: bold;">What's New in this Release</span>

*   **Replace Media Modification **– Additional logic around unpublishing media during replace media action, was added.

When replacing media action is taking place:

*   If media is published in a moderated channel/category - Media will be unpublished and moved to pending moderation state
*   If media is in un-moderated channel/category - Media will still be published

In addition, the comment in 'replace media' tab was changed to reflect that and a note was added: "media will be unpublished from a moderated location (channel/gallery/category) and will remain published otherwise"

<p class="mce-heading-3">
  Version 5.20.157<a name="v5_20_157"></a>
</p>

These release notes pertain to Kaltura MediaSpace 5.20.157, released April 6, 2015.

 <a name="V_5_9_04" style="color: #828a8c; font-size: 14pt; font-weight: bold; background-color: #ffffff;"></a><span style="color: #828a8c; font-size: 14pt; font-weight: bold;">What's New in this Release</span>

*   **Audio Entry Configuration **– Configuration to set different embed size for custom audio player was added in KMS admin. In *Audioentry* module a field called *embedSizes* was added. Note that this setting requires a custom player (in *customPlayerId* field). if custom player won't be givven, the audio entry will be by default as the video entry player.

<p class="mce-heading-3">
  <a name="v5_20_107"></a>Version 5.20.107
</p>

These release notes pertain to Kaltura MediaSpace 5.20.107, released March 22, 2015.

 <a name="V_5_9_04" style="color: #828a8c; font-size: 14pt; font-weight: bold; background-color: #ffffff;"></a><span style="color: #828a8c; font-size: 14pt; font-weight: bold;">What's New in this Release</span>

*   **Media Collaboration **– Enable media owners to add co-editors and co-publishers to their media or to change the media owner altogether. Co-editors can edit entry's details and metadata, trim media, replace media, edit captions, edit chapters and slides (cannot delete media or add new co-editors and co-publishers). Co-Publisher can publish the media to their entitled Categories or Channels. The KMS admin can enable this feature in *MediaCollaboration* module.
*   Note that if configuration will be set to 'no' after it was set to 'yes' and in the meantime some entries were added with co-editors and co-publisher, all co-editors and co-publishers will lose their ability to view, edit or publish the entries they took action on.
*   Note that change owner feature has special configuration than co-editor/co-publisher and can be set to enable or disable without any dependency on the other two. The KMS admin do this in configuration field *changeOwnerEnabled* (which appears once *mediaCollaborationEnabled* is set to 'yes')   
    Read more [here][9].

 [9]: http://knowledge.kaltura.com/media-collaboration

<p class="mce-heading-3">
  <a name="v5_20_06"></a>Version 5.20.06
</p>

These release notes pertain to Kaltura MediaSpace 5.20.06, released March 9, 2015.

 

<p class="mce-heading-3">
  <a name="V_5_9_04"></a><span>What's New in this Release</span>
</p>

*   **Channels Sort Default **– The KMS admin can choose default sort method for the channels list in channels page - Media Count, Alphabetical, Members and Subscribers or Most Recent. The field *channelsSorting* was added under *channels* module.

<p class="mce-heading-3">
  <a name="V_5_19"></a>Version 5.19.12
</p>

These release notes pertain to Kaltura MediaSpace 5.19.12, released March 2, 2015.

 <a name="V_5_9_04" style="color: #828a8c; font-size: 14pt; font-weight: bold; background-color: #ffffff;"></a><span style="color: #828a8c; font-size: 14pt; font-weight: bold;">What's New in this Release</span>

*   **Download Media** – Media owners in KMS and KAF applications can configure downloadable versions of the media for viewers to download from the media page. KMS admin can configure this feature under *downloadmedia *module. Read more [here][10].
*   **Media Analytics** – Media owners can view analytics on their media - Total plays, views, plays in channels, plays in categories, users that watched and more. This new page is avaialbe to them from the 'Actions' drop down of the entry page. KMS admin can configure this feature under *userreports* module, *mediaAnalytics* field. Entry analytics in this report is identical to the analytiics for the entry in the KMC.

 [10]: http://knowledge.kaltura.com/download-media

 <a name="V5_17_07" style="background-color: #ffffff;"></a><span style="color: #828a8c; font-size: 14pt; font-weight: bold;">Version 5.18.10</span>

These release notes pertain to Kaltura MediaSpace 5.18.10, released February 9, 2015.

<p class="mce-heading-3">
  <a name="V_5_9_04"></a><span>What's New in this Release</span>
</p>

*   **Replace Media** – Media owners can now replace their media, while keeping metadata, URL and analytics in place. The same functionality as in the KMC is now available in KMS and is configurable by the KMS admin under the  *replacemedia* module. Note that only video entries can be replaced. Any time-based metadata on the entry will be kept in place and will probably be out of sync with the new media, and should be manually adjusted.
*   **Attached Files** – Media owners can now attach files of any type to their media, enabling media viewers to download the file before, during or after viewing. This feature can be enabled by the KMS admin under the *Attachments* module. 
*   **Audio Entries Thumbnail** – Audio entries now have a player thumbnail similar to video entries.

<p class="mce-heading-3">
  <a name="V5_17_07"></a>Version 5.17.07
</p>

These release notes pertain to Kaltura MediaSpace 5.17.07, released January 25, 2015.

<a name="V_5_9_04" style="color: #828a8c; font-size: 14pt; font-weight: bold; background-color: #ffffff;"></a><span style="color: #828a8c; font-size: 14pt; font-weight: bold;">What's New in this Release</span>

*   **Chapters and Slides **– A new configurable module that enables adding, editing and viewing Chapters and Slides on a media entry is now available. The basic configuration of enable/disable is under *Chapters* module in KMS Admin. Note that the minimum edit and view players version required for this module to work is 2.26. To learn more visit [here][11].
*   **Audio Entries are displayed on the default KMS player** - Audio entries are  now being displayed inside MediaSpace pages on the default view player (large player and not slim one with just the scrubber like before).

 [11]: http://knowledge.kaltura.com/mediaspace-chapters-and-slides-module

 <span style="color: #828a8c; font-size: 14pt; font-weight: bold;">Resolved Issues</span>

<p class="mce-heading-3">
  <a name="V5_16_10"></a>Version 5.16.10<span> </span>
</p>

These release notes pertain to Kaltura MediaSpace 5.16.10, released January 11, 2015.

<a name="V_5_9_04" style="color: #828a8c; font-size: 14pt; font-weight: bold; background-color: #ffffff;"></a><span style="color: #828a8c; font-size: 14pt; font-weight: bold;">What's New in this Release</span>

*   **Mobile Related Fixes** – A new iOS Mobile App package (v0.71) was created and soon to be public in the Apple store (submitted and now on Apple's approval process). The new package introduce bug fixes and no new functionality. In addition, on the Kaltura MeediaSpace side, some mobile related issues (for both Mobile App and Mobile browser view) were fixed. see all the fixes in the list below, marked as 'Mobile App'.
*   **Channel Analytics text changes** - In the channel analytics page, on the Dashboard tab, some text changes and additions were done in order to clarify the data and the UX.

1.  'Played' text was changed to 'Viewed'
2.  Tooltips were added

*   **Cielo24 module was added to KMS Admin** - Cielo24 module, for automatic captioning and metadata extraction (licensed module) was added to KMS admin console. In order to activate please contact your Kaltura representative or support. Read more [here][12].

 [12]: http://exchange.kaltura.com/content/cielo24-searchable-captions

<p class="mce-heading-3">
  <a name="V_5_9_04"></a><span>Version 5.15.06</span>
</p>

These release notes pertain to Kaltura MediaSpace 5.15.06, released December 28, 2014.

<span style="color: #828a8c; font-size: 14pt; font-weight: bold;">What's New in this Release</span>

*   **Playlist Management Changes – **The user experience changes were applied to ‘add to playlist’ workflow, on entry page, My Media and My Playlist pages. Texts and components’ location was changed but functionality was not added or removed. No configuration is needed in order to view these changes.
*   Playlist checkbox list was changed from horizontal to vertical view
*   Button text was changed from "manage playlist" to "go to My Playlists" and was moved to the right side
*   The text was changed from ‘add to playlist’ to ‘create new playlist’ inside the text box
*   Button text was changed from 'add' to 'create'
*   ‘Select Playlists’ headline was added to the checkboxes area
*   ‘Save’ button and action was added to adding and removing from playlist workflow
*   The option to delete playlist (x sign) from the playlists blue tags was removed

*   **Enhancements to Channel Analytics **– Additional data and options were added to Channel analytics screens. No configuration is needed to in order to view this new data.

*   A new time range was added to the reports, a custom range. Enables the user to select a specific time range for the report and not just ‘last 7/30/etc days’
*   A trend was added to the dashboard data – On the Played/Plays and User Watched/Contributed data, a red/green percentage was added to show the change from the previous period selected in the time range.
*   In Media report a column with small graph of last 7 days plays for each entry was added (number of plays of this entry in the channel)
*   In Engagement report a column with small graph of last 7 days plays for each user was added (number of plays of this user in the channel)
*   In Media Report, "Plays" column text was changed to "Plays in Channel" and another columns called "Total Plays" was added to the right of it. This new column shows all plays of the entry regardless of the context (the channel). This will show the channel manager the ration between channel plays and general plays of the entry.

<p class="mce-heading-3">
  <a name="v5_14_7"></a>Version 5.14.07
</p>

<p class="mce-heading-3">
  <a name="V_5_9_04"></a>
</p>

These release notes pertain to Kaltura MediaSpace 5.14.07, released December 14, 2014.

<span style="color: #828a8c; font-size: 14pt; font-weight: bold;">What's New in this Release</span>

1.  **Search on Custom Metadata **- Search results now show entries with matching text from custom metadata fields and not only basic metadata (title, description, text). Searchable custom metadata fields are of text type, at the moment. Results will include '+' sign that shows the custom metadata fields and the matching one will be highlighted. No admin configuration is required for this feature.
2.  **Homepage playlist links to a playlist page -** Playlists in the homepage ('most recent', 'most popular', etc.) showing 9 entries, are now clickable, leading to a playlist media page with the full list of playlist entries. All playlist (default and custom, manual and rule-based) that can be placed in the homepage will get this functionality. No admin configuration is required for that.
3.  **Search for categories in media publishing workflow **- When publishing an entry the users can choose publishing destination, Channels or Categories, both presented in different tabs. In Channels tab there is a search box to find the desired destination from the entire list and now in Categories tab a search box was added. Results of the search will be highlighted on the category tree. No admin configuration is required for that.

<p class="mce-heading-3">
  <a name="v5_13_06"></a>Version 5.13.06
</p>

<p class="mce-heading-3">
  <a name="V_5_9_04"></a>
</p>

These release notes pertain to Kaltura MediaSpace 5.13.06, released November 30, 2014.

<span style="color: #828a8c; font-size: 14pt; font-weight: bold;">What's New in this Release</span>

1.  **Email Share **– End-users can share Kaltura unlisted and published media via Email. This is available in share tab, like media grab embed and page link. The media will be shared by the default mail client on the machine. The admin can configure this feature in ‘embed’ module and it will have same settings as embed module (embedAllowed).
2.  **Twitter Cards** – Twitting media URL makes it visible and playable in Kaltura player within Twitter (similar to KMS Facebook Tags module). The admin can configure this feature in ‘twitter’ module and must input player ID and Twitter @username that the site will use. In order to use this feature ‘allowAnonymous’ in ‘auth’ module must be enabled as well and 'Default Entitlement Enforcement' on the partner should be disabled  (same as in Facebook module).
3.  **Public Channel** – A new type of channel that allows anonymous users (guests) to view this channel (which is blocked for other channels) and the content published to it. When enabled, Channels gallery link will be available to anonymous users as well, but showing only public channels. The admin can configure this feature in ‘channels’ module under ‘suportPublicChannel’. In order to use this feature ‘allowAnonymous’ in ‘auth’ module must be enabled as well.

<p class="mce-heading-3">
  <a name="v5_11_05"></a>Version 5.11.05
</p>

<p class="mce-heading-3">
  <a name="V_5_9_04"></a>
</p>

These release notes pertain to Kaltura MediaSpace 5.11.05, released August 10, 2014.

<span style="color: #828a8c; font-size: 14pt; font-weight: bold;">What's New in this Release</span>

*   **Update Channel Thumbnail** - MediaSpace Channel Managers can set the thumbnail of their choice to their channels. This feature is available to all MediaSpace users. For more information see <a href="http://knowledge.kaltura.com/node/1237" target="_blank">here</a>.
*   **Playlist Secure Embed **- MediaSpace administrators can now set the playlist embed to be secure (similarly to entry secure embed). MediaSpace entitlements will be enforced on a playlist that is embedded in external sites. When embedding a playlist to your sites and blogs, you will be prompted to authenticate (if not already authenticated). If a user is authorized to watch the media according to the entitlements defined in MediaSpace, the media will play. Otherwise, a message is displayed indicating that the user is not authorized to watch the media. Note that if playlist secure embed is not enabled, only public media is viewable in the playlist, However, when the playlist secure embed is enabled, you will be required to login (to display the addtional media aside from the public media of the playlist). Playlist secure embed cannot work when anonymous MediaSpace is enabled. Activate this feature in the *KMS Admin > Embedplaylist* module and set* secureEmbed to *Yes.
*   **Kaltura Screen Recorder Troubleshooting Guide** - Since the Kaltura Screen Recorder uses Java which may cause issues on certain devices and browsers, a clarification note was added in the screen recording media creation. The note states that "The Kaltura Sscreen Recorder uses Java which has certain limitations on certain devices and browsers. For more information see <a href="http://knowledge.kaltura.com/how-troubleshoot-kaltura-screen-recorder#ksr+safari" target="_blank">here</a>". We intend to add an option for MediaSpace Admins to enable/disable this note and to edit the text and link as they wish to.

<a name="V_5_8_07"></a><a name="V_5_9_04"></a><a name="v_5_10_06"></a>

<p class="mce-heading-3">
  Version 5.10.06<span> </span>
</p>

<p class="mce-heading-3">
  <a name="V_5_9_04"></a>
</p>

These release notes pertain to Kaltura MediaSpace 5.10.06, released July 27, 2014.

<span style="color: #828a8c; font-size: 14pt; font-weight: bold;">What's New in this Release</span>

*   **Add YouTube External Entry into MediaSpace** - MediaSpace users can add YouTube video content and metadata into MediaSpace. Hosted content on YouTube is played back on the Kaltura V2 player from version 2.13 and above. To update player to the latest player version,  re-save the player settings in the *KMC Studio > Universal Studio *tab). MediaSpace administrators can activate the YouTube module in the *KMS Admin *by selecting* YouTube* module.
*   **View modes for Galleries** - MediaSpace administrators can define optional view modes for media items inside Galleries. Activate this feature in the *KMS Admin > Gallery* module. In* categoryDefaultView* choose from Grid, Collaped view or Detailed view.
*   **Terms of Agreement before Uploading or Publishing content** - MediaSpace administrators can enforce the Terms of Agreement text and checkbox for end-users to review and/or accept before uploading or publishing content. Activate this in *KMS Admin* > *Disclaimer *module.
*   **'Kaltura Auto' is the default playback option for a new MediaSpace instance** - 'Kaltura Auto' chooses between HTTP Progressive Download and Akamai’s HTTP Adaptive Streaming, based on the entry duration and available flavors. 'Kaltura Auto' gives you the best video delivery and playback quality for your entry. This option is configured in the KMS Admin under player/playback.

<a name="V_5_8_07_MAIN"></a><span class="mce-heading-3">Version 5.8.07</span>

These release notes pertain to Kaltura MediaSpace 5.8.07, released May 18, 2014.

<p class="mce-heading-3">
  What's New in this Release
</p>

*   ****G**lobal search results default sort order** – MediaSpace administrators can now choose the default sort order for global search results. To define the default order, in your *KMS Admin > Gallery* module, configure the desired value for **globalSearchSortMediaBy**.
*   **Kaltura Server CDN URL Configuration **- MediaSpace administrators can now change the Kaltura Server CDN URL used by the Kaltura HTML5 player and player embeds. The default value is http://cdnapi.kaltura.com. To update your CDN URL, in your *KMS Admin > Client* module, add the URL in **CDNUrl**.   
    <span>Note</span>: When configuring a KMS site to HTTPS, also change the CDN URL to **https://cdnapisec.kaltura.com**.
*   **Create Clip button in the Edit Media page **- A new "Create Clip" feature now allows media owners to create clips directly from the Edit Media page. To add the button to the Edit Media page, enable the *KMS Admin > Clipper* module.

<p class="mce-heading-3">
  <a name="April27"></a><a name="V_5_7_251"></a><span>Version 5.7.251</span><span> </span>
</p>

These release notes pertain to Kaltura MediaSpace 5.7.251, released May 4, 2014.

<span style="color: #666560; font-size: 12pt; font-weight: bold;">What's New in this Release</span>

*   **Added support for Arabic - **MediaSpace administrators can now select Arabic as their MediaSpace language. From *Application > Language*, select ar.

<span style="color: #666560; font-size: 12pt; font-weight: bold;">Resolved Issues</span>

<p class="mce-heading-3">
  <a name="April27"></a>Version 5.7.204
</p>

These release notes pertain to Kaltura MediaSpace 5.7.204, released April 27, 2014.

<span style="color: #666560; font-size: 12pt; font-weight: bold;">What's New in this Release</span>

*   **Header Menu Links Location**<span> – </span>MediaSpace administrators can now choose the location of where each added link will appear. Added links can be displayed in the header itself (as they did before) or in the user drop down menu that is part of the header (for example, “My Media”, “My Playlists, etc.). To define the location of your menu items of type URL, in your KMS Admin > Headermenu module, configure the **linkLocation **for each menu of type URL.

*   **Default Media Privacy** - MediaSpace administrators can now define the default privacy for each newly uploaded media. Prior to this change, each newly uploaded media's status was set  to  "Private" as the default. Now, MediaSpace administrators can configure every newly uploaded media to be set as "Unlisted" by default, and allow the media owner to change the privacy mode. To configure this option, from your KMS Admin > Publish module set the required value for **defaultPublishStatusOnUpload**. Note that this configuration is applicable only if Unlisted mode is enabled on your MediaSpace instance. You can check if it is enabled under Application > enableUnlisted.**  
    **

<p class="mce-heading-3">
  <a name="April6"></a>Version 5.7.153
</p>

These release notes pertain to Kaltura MediaSpace 5.7.153,  released April 6, 2014.

<span style="color: #666560; font-size: 12pt; font-weight: bold;">What's New in this Release</span>

*   **Playback Options** - MediaSpace administrators can now select additional playback options. From *Player > playback*, select any of the following options:
*   **Auto** - Kaltura server chooses between HTTP Progressive Download and Akamai’s HTTP Adaptive Streaming, based on entry duration and available flavors. Auto gives you the best video delivery and playback quality for your entry.
*   **HTTP Progressive Download** – Allows you to pause the video playback and wait for the content to download. Typically used where viewers have very limited bandwidth and might experience more buffering than adaptive bitrate.
*   **HTTP Streaming (HDS)** - HTTP streaming based on Adobe technology. Allows adaptive bitrate so the player can adjust the video quality on the fly based on network and CPU conditions.
*   **HTTP Streaming (Akamai HD)** – HTTP streaming based on Akamai’s technology. Allows adaptive bitrate so the player can adjust the video quality on the fly based on network and CPU conditions, formally called Akamai HD.
*   **RTMP Streaming** – RTMP streaming based on Adobe technology. Allows adaptive bitrate so the player can adjust the video quality on the fly based on network and CPU conditions.
*   **Secure Transport (RTMPE)** - RTMP encrypted using Adobe's security mechanism which wraps the RTMP session in a lighter-weight encryption layer.

<p class="mce-heading-3">
  <a name="Mar23"></a>Version 5.7.104
</p>

These release notes pertain to Kaltura MediaSpace 5.7.104,  released March 23, 2014. 

<span style="color: #666560; font-size: 12pt; font-weight: bold;">What's New in this Release</span>

*   **Portuguese Localization** - MediaSpace administrators can now select Portuguese as their MediaSpace language. From *Application > Language*, select **pt-br**.
*   **Upload Files over 2GB** - MediaSpace now supports uploading files that are larger than 2GB. Note that this is supported in Chrome, Safari, Firefox and IE 10+.
*   **Static Pages** - MediaSpace administrators can now add static/content pages to their MediaSpace site. These pages can be used, for example, to create help pages, privacy policies etc. From the KMS Admin, enable the *Staticpages* module. After you enable the module, you can add multiple pages to your site. Each page should include:

*   Title - The title of your page to display as the page header
*   Page 'slug' - The unique identifier for the page to be accessed as a URL. For example, if you provide 'privacy' as a slug, you can add links to your static page as *[MediaSpace URL]/privacy*. You can add these links in Navigation or Headermenu modules or anywhere you want to include links to your pages within the MediaSpace site.
*   Permission - Which role and above can access the page.
*   Content - The content of the page to display. You can use <a href="http://www.w3schools.com/html/" target="_blank">HTML</a> markup and <a href="http://getbootstrap.com/2.3.2/base-css.html" target="_blank">Bootstrap</a> markup. 

*   **Offline Download** - This feature allows MediaSpace native application users to download media and view offline when there is no connectivity. To enable this feature, from your KMS Admin, go to *Native > enableOffline* = **Yes** and list the flavors that you would like to allow to download to mobile devices. Note that in order to use the <a href="http://corp.kaltura.com/Products/Video-Applications/Kaltura-Native-Mobile-App" target="_blank">MediaSpace Native Application</a> an additional feature is required on your MediaSpace instance. If you are interested to try the MediaSpace native application, please contact your customer success manager.

<p class="mce-heading-3">
  <a name="March9"></a>Version 5.7.52
</p>

These release notes pertain to Kaltura MediaSpace 5.7.52,  released March 9, 2014. 

<span style="color: #666560; font-size: 12pt; font-weight: bold;">What's New in this Release</span>

*   **Add <a href="http://www.walkme.com/" target="_blank">WalkMe</a> Walk-Thru Guidance - **MediaSpace administrators can now configure their MediaSpace instance to use their own WalkMe account and walkthroughs and configure MediaSpace to always load the guides for their MediaSpace users. From *KMS Admin > Walkmethru* module, add you own WalkMe JS URL to *scriptUrl* and leave the *activationParam* field empty.
*   **Show Comments in Channels Only** - Show comments on media entries to users only in the context of a channel. In this case, users will not be able to see media comments if browsing to the media from search results, my media or any other context that doesn't include the context of the channel. To enable this feature, from the *KMS Admin > Comments* set *showInChannelsOnly* to **Yes**.
*   **Publish Immidiately When Adding New Media to Channel/Category** -  When creating a new webcam or screen recording through "Add Media" in a channel or category, the media is published automatically to the channel/category. Previously, this was the case only when uploading new media.

<p class="mce-heading-3">
  <a name="Feb9"></a>Version 5.6.05
</p>

These release notes pertain to Kaltura MediaSpace 5.6.05,  released February 9, 2014. 

<p class="mce-heading-4">
  What's New in this Release
</p>

*   **Publish live streams to channels and categories** - Live streams that are provisioned from the KMC can be published and displayed in any channel or category. The streams are also found in search results. If the live entry is associated with the user ID of a MediaSpace user, it will be available from the media owner through "My Media", to manage and publish from MediaSpace.
*   **Provision a Live Event and Stream from MediaSpace** -  Authorized MediaSpace users can create a live event from MediaSpace that is provisioned instantaneously. Users are able to stream from MediaSpace using a web camera without the need for external encoding software.

**NOTE:** Provisioning a live event from MediaSpace requires the new Kaltura Live feature to be enabled on your partner. This feature is currently in limited avaialbility only and will be offered to selected customers during this time. See [Live Streaming Using Kaltura Live Streaming (HDS / HLS / DASH)][14] for more information.

 [14]: http://knowledge.kaltura.com/node/1047

Using live in MediaSpace requires you to update the uiConf of your main player to SWF URL version 3.9.7 or above.

<p class="mce-heading-3">
  <a name="Jan26"></a>Version 5.5.05
</p>

These release notes pertain to Kaltura MediaSpace 5.5.05,  released January 26, 2014. 

<p class="mce-heading-4">
  What's New in this Release
</p>

*   **Enhanced Moderation Control** - MediaSpace administrators can now define whether new channels that are created should be moderated by default. In addition, MediaSpace administrators can configure if the moderation option can be disabled by channel managers, to comply with use cases where moderation must be enforced. In the *Channelmoderation* module, you can set the *moderationDefaultValue* to define if the moderation option should be enabled or not by default when channels are created. The *forceModeration* parameter, in the same module, removes the checkbox from the channel creation form, allowing the MediaSpace administrator to control the moderation configuration centrally.
*   **Terms of Use and Disclaimer Messages**
*   **Channel Creation **- MediaSpace administrators can now configure a policy message that is displayed to users every time a channel is created. To configure a policy message, in the *Channels* module, you can set a value for the *channelsTermUse* parameter. The configured text is displayed in the top of the channel creation form.
*   **Add Member to Channel** - MediaSpace administrators can configure a disclaimer message that is displayed to channel managers when adding members to the channel. To set the disclaimer, in the *Channelmembers* module, set the value of *addMemberGuidelines*. The configured message is displayed in the Add Member form.
*   **Policy Message for Users** - MediaSpace administrators can now configure a policy message that is displayed to all users. The policy message is displayed when watching videos, next to the player, and when browsing content in a channel, under the channel info box. To configure this message, enable the *Contentpolicy* module and add the policy message to the *contentPolicyText* parameter. 

*   **Helper Description for Metadata Fields** - MediaSpace administrators can now set helper messages that are displayed next to each metadata field, to guide users when uploading or editing media. To set the description for the media Name, Description and Tags, under the *Metadata* module you can configure text for the parameters: *basicNameFieldHelperText*, *basicDescriptionFieldHelperText *and *basicTagsFieldHelperText* respectively. To display helper text custom metadata fields, make sure to enter a *Description* for each field in the custom data schema via the KMC.*  
    *

<p class="mce-heading-3">
  <a name="Jan12"></a>Version 5.4.53
</p>

These release notes pertain to Kaltura MediaSpace 5.4.53,  released January 12, 2014. 

<span style="color: #666560; font-size: 12pt; font-weight: bold;">What's New in this Release</span>

*   **Clipping and Trimming** - Media owners and users can now edit videos in the cloud. Media owners can trim videos that were previously uploaded and replace the current media. In addition, media owners can define the videos that other users can generate clips from. To enable this feature, enable the *Clipper* module in your KMS Admin.
*   **Auto-complete Tags** - The 'Tags' field automatically completes values from tags that already exist in your application. This allows you to consolidate taxonomy and improve discoverability of your content.
*   **Default Channel Type** - MediaSpace administrators can now configure the default channel type that is created when users create a new channel. To configure the default channel type, set the value of *defaultChannelType* under KMS Admin > Channels.
*   **Home Page Carousel Enhancements** - You can now select the style of the home page carousel. In your KMS Admin, under Home > *carouselStyle*, you can select either a style where a single entry is displayed with a cropped image accross the entire width of the screen, or a style that displays the current entry in its orignal aspect ratio, plus a portion of the previous and next entries. 
*   **Media Share URL** - The URL to share media in the context of a channel now includes the context ID of the channel itself. The channel analytics for views that result in sharing the URL via email or other methods are tracked properly.

<p class="mce-heading-3">
  <a name="Jan5"></a>Version 5.4.03
</p>

These release notes pertain to Kaltura MediaSpace 5.4.03,  released January 5, 2014.  
<span style="color: #666560; font-size: 12pt; font-weight: bold;">What's New in this Release</span>

*   **Private Channel Comments**: Channel managers can configure to keep all comments that are added in the context of a channel, private, even if the commented media is published in other channels. To enable this feature, in your KMS Admin > Comments, set *showPrivateCommentsConfig* to *Yes*. After this option is set, the new option is visible to channel managers in the Edit Channel Options page.
*   **Comments with Time Markers**: Users can now comment on videos and reference a specific time frame in the video. To enable this feature, in your KMS Admin > Comments, set  *setshowAddTimedCommentsCheckbox* to *Yes*. This allows you to select to add the time marker using a checkbox or to simply enter a time stamp in the comment itself. There is no need for a special markup, just enter the time reference as MM:SS or HH:MM:SS.

<p class="mce-heading-3">
  <a name="Dec1"></a>Version 5.3.9
</p>

These release notes pertain to Kaltura MediaSpace 5.3.9,  released December 1, 2013. 

<span style="color: #666560; font-size: 12pt; font-weight: bold;">What's New in this Release</span>

*   **Home Page Enhancements:**
*   **Thumbnails - **Thumbnails are now displayed in their original size and the carousel also displays a portion of the previous and next media items.
*   **Indicators** - The carousel inlucdes indicators that display how many items the carousel contains, as well as indicators that allow you to navigate between items and highlight the current one.
*   **Interval** - You can configure the interval that the carousel slides items. In the *Home* module, you cna set *carouselInterval* (in msec).

*   **Shared Repositories Enhancements**
*   **Terms of Agreement** - (Optional)  You can define a Terms of Agreement that users must agree to before contributing media to a shared repository. In the *SharedRepositories* module configuration add a URL for *termsOfUseLink*.
*   **Metadata Schema** - The KMS admin can configure an additional schema that is applicable only for media added to Shared Repositories , including which fields from the schema are required before media can be published there. In the *SharedRepositories* module configuration select a metadata schema under *customDataProfileId* and optionally, select which fields are required under *requiredFields*.

*   **Thumbnail Management** - You can upload thumbnails for your media entries from MediaSpace through the Thumbnails tab. Additional available options are: capture from a frame in the video, select one thumbnail out of 10 that are generated randomly, download current default thumbnail. To enable this feature, enable the *Thumbnails* module from your KMS Admin.
*   **Player Configuration** - The ability to define the relative height of the player used in MediaSpace has been added, to ensure that it is displayed appropriately in the web responsive design The aspect ratio of the content in your MediaSpace site is maintained. In your KMS Admin, under *Player* you can set teh value of *playerVideoRatioPercent*. 
*   **Search Enhancements**:
*   You can configure whether the global search is displayed in the header or sliding navigation panel. This can be configured from the KMS Admin under *Navigation* > *showSearchBoxInHeader*
*   The Category/Channel search shows as a collapsed icon in the page tabs to better differentiate the global search.

<p class="mce-heading-3">
  <a name="Nov3"></a>Version 5.2.8
</p>

These release notes pertain to Kaltura MediaSpace 5.2.8,  released November 3, 2013. 

<span style="color: #666560; font-size: 12pt; font-weight: bold;">What's New in this Release</span>

*   **Mobile Upload** - You can now upload images and video files directly from your phone and tablet browser using the <a href="https://github.com/kaltura/jQuery-File-Upload" target="_blank">new upload control</a> that uploads files in chunks and supports resuming uploads as well. Note: not all features are supported on all mobile browsers and operating system versions. Please refer to <a href="https://github.com/blueimp/jQuery-File-Upload/wiki/Browser-support" target="_blank">this list</a> for detailed information.
*   **Shared Repositories** - You can create shared media repositories that allow any member to not only browse the media that is published in the shared repository, but also use the media to publish to other channels and/or categories. This new type of repository allows education institutions and enterprises to create a shared media location for media that anyone with access to it has publishing rights to other areas in MediaSpace. Enable the *SharedRepositories* module from your KMS Admin.
*   **Channel Analytics** - Channel Managers can now measure and analyze the user engagement and contribution to their channels. These contextual analytics allow channel managers to answer important questions such as: What are the most popular videos in the channel? Who are the members that watch the most videos and what is their drop off rate? Who are the members that contribute the most media to the channel? To enable this feature, enable the *Userreports* modulefrom the KMS Admin .
*   **Enhanced Control over Channel Creation** - You can define which role can create specific channel types (open, restricted, private and shared repository). This capability provides better control if you are trying to control who can create public and or private areas in MediaSpace. In your KMS Admin, under *Channels* you can separately set values for *channelCreatorOpen*, *channelCreatorRestricted*, *channelCreatorPrivate* and *channelCreatorSharedRepository.* 
*   **Webcam Recording Enhacements** - The Webcam authoring tool was updated to support higher quality video recording. In your KMS Admin, under Widgets set *krecordDefaults* to *Yes, to *expose additional fields to configure the webcam widget quality.

<p class="mce-heading-3">
  <a name="October13"></a>Version 5.1.5 
</p>

These release notes pertain to Kaltura MediaSpace 5.1.5,  released October 13, 2013. 

<span style="color: #666560; font-size: 12pt; font-weight: bold;">What's New in this Release</span>

*   **Localization** - You can now choose Spanish, French or German from the MediaSpace Admin to localize your MediaSpace site. In your KMS Admin, under *Application* you can set the *language* value. 
*   **Unlisted Media - **The URL to your media can be shared without the need to publish it to a category or channel. For each of your media entries, you can now select if the entry should be private, unlisted or published (to specific categories and/or channels). Unlisted media can be accessed by anyone with a direct link to the media page and will not show in search results. To enable this feature, in your KMS Admin under *Application*, you can set  *enableUnlisted*.
*   **Secured Embed Code** - MediaSpace entitlements are now enforced on media that is embeded in external sites. When embeding restricted or private media to your sites and blogs, you will be prompted to authenticate (if not already authenticated). If a user is authorized to watch the media according to the entitlements defined in MediaSpace, the media will play. Otherwise, a message will be displayed that they are not authorized to watch the media. To enable this feature, from your KMS Admin > *Embed* module set *secureEmbed* to *Yes*.
*   **Publish from Upload Page** - You can now select the privacy settings for your added media from the upload page itself. When adding new media and editing the metadata, you can also select if the media will be private, unlisted or automatically published to specific categories and/or channels when the media is ready.
*   **Swipe Gestures for Home Page Carousel** - You can use swipe gestures in your home page carousel when accessing MediaSpace on your mobile device browser or MediaSpace native app.

<span><span class="mce-heading-2"><span class="mce-heading-3"><a name="v5_0_105"></a>Version 5.0.105</span></span></span>These release notes pertain to Kaltura MediaSpace 5.0.105,  released September 29, 2013. 

<span style="color: #666560; font-size: 12pt; font-weight: bold;">What's New in this Release</span>

*   **Navigation Menu Layout** - You can configure the Navigation menu layout on the desktop view to be either:
*   Vertical - Sliding panel that supports unlimited number of sub categories
*   Horizontal - Horizontal bar under the header with a limited number of sub categories

<p style="padding-left: 30px;">
  To set the style, from your KMS Admin > <em>Navigation</em> module, set the <em>navigationStyle</em> value.
</p>

*   **User Attributes in SSO Gateway** - Added the ability to pass multiple user atttributes in the SSO gateway such as first name, last name, email, etc.

<p class="mce-heading-3">
  <a name="Aug25"></a>Version 5.0.55 
</p>

These release notes pertain to the Kaltura MediaSpace 5.0.55 released August 25, 2013. 

<span style="color: #828a8c; font-size: 14pt; font-weight: bold;">What's New in this Release</span>

<table border="1" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
  <thead>
    <tr>
      <td valign="top" width="120">
        <p class="TableHeading">
          <strong>Feature</strong>
        </p>
      </td>
      
      <td valign="bottom">
        <p class="TableHeading">
          <strong>Description</strong>
        </p>
      </td>
    </tr>
  </thead>
  
  <tbody>
    <tr>
      <td valign="top">
        <p>
          Cross device experience on any screen size and shape 
        </p>
      </td>
      
      <td style="text-align: left;" valign="top" width="300">
        <ul>
          <li>
            Built on top of <a href="http://getbootstrap.com/" target="_blank">Bootstrap</a> - the leading responsive web design framework 
          </li>
          <li>
            Automatically adjusts site layout to the screen size and device
          </li>
          <li>
            Support for gestures and infinite scrolling
          </li>
        </ul>
      </td>
    </tr>
    
    <tr>
      <td valign="top" width="120">
        <p>
          Easier skinning and branding of your MediaSpace site
        </p>
      </td>
      
      <td style="text-align: left;" valign="top" width="300">
        <ul>
          <li>
            Create your own standard Bootstrap CSS by leveraging free tools that don't require coding and upload it via the MediaSpace admin site
          </li>
          <li>
            Choose one of the 14 <a href="http://bootswatch.com/" target="_blank">open source Boostrap CSS files</a> included with this release
          </li>
        </ul>
      </td>
    </tr>
    
    <tr>
      <td valign="top" width="120">
        <p>
          Granular delegation of ownership and permissions over content and site sections
        </p>
      </td>
      
      <td style="text-align: left;" valign="top" width="300">
        <ul>
          <li>
            Granular permissions and user management on a channel and category level
          </li>
          <li>
            Inherit permissions from parent categories
          </li>
          <li>
            Import members from parent categories
          </li>
          <li>
            Synchronize channel and category members with your own group management server 
          </li>
          <li>
            Moderate content in channels and categories
          </li>
          <li>
            Enhanced moderation to easily review and approve content
          </li>
        </ul>
      </td>
    </tr>
    
    <tr>
      <td valign="top" width="120">
        <p>
          Enhanced navigation and site structure
        </p>
      </td>
      
      <td style="text-align: left;" valign="top" width="300">
        <ul>
          <li>
            Unified navigation - Each category / sub category can include media and channels
          </li>
          <li>
            Sliding navigation panel to support unlimited number of sub categories and easy navigation
          </li>
        </ul>
      </td>
    </tr>
    
    <tr>
      <td valign="top" width="120">
        <p>
          Dedicated experience for every media type
        </p>
      </td>
      
      <td style="text-align: left;" valign="top" width="300">
        <ul>
          <li>
            Dedicated playback experience for video, audio and images
          </li>
          <li>
            Enhanced View Media page with all the essential functionality   
          </li>
        </ul>
      </td>
    </tr>
    
    <tr>
      <td valign="top" width="120">
        <p>
          Home page module to engage your audience from the start
        </p>
      </td>
      
      <td style="text-align: left;" valign="top" width="300">
        <ul>
          <li>
            Display featured content in a carousel
          </li>
          <li>
            Curate and feature media on your home page using a static or dynamic playlist (most popular, most liked, most recent, most commented, etc.)
          </li>
        </ul>
      </td>
    </tr>
    
    <tr>
      <td valign="top" width="120">
        <p>
          Reach international audiences in their local langage
        </p>
      </td>
      
      <td style="text-align: left;" valign="top" width="300">
         Localized MediaSpace user interface and metadata in:<br /><ul>
          <li>
            Spanish
          </li>
          <li>
            German
          </li>
          <li>
            French
          </li>
        </ul>
      </td>
    </tr>
    
    <tr>
      <td valign="top" width="120">
        <p>
          Enhanced User Experience
        </p>
      </td>
      
      <td style="text-align: left;" valign="top" width="300">
        <ul>
          <li>
            Easily search on metadata, in-video search (closed caption files and transcripts), channels and categories
          </li>
          <li>
            Enhanced My Media section to easily filter media by its status and see where each media is published and/or pending moderation
          </li>
          <li>
            Enhanced Publish module to easily search channels and find channels that you manage or can contribute to 
          </li>
          <li>
            Enhanced Channel page allowing channel managers to create their own "mini-portal"
          </li>
          <li>
            WYSIWYG editor for media, channel and category description to input rich text
          </li>
          <li>
            Show the user's display name accross the entire site (thumbnails, comments, etc.)
          </li>
        </ul>
      </td>
    </tr>
  </tbody>
</table>

<span style="color: #484848; font-size: 18pt; font-weight: bold;">Version 5.51.12</span>

These release notes pertain to Kaltura MediaSpace 5.51.12, expected to be released on September 12, 2016. 

<p class="mce-heading-3">
  What's New in This Release
</p>

*   **oEmbed Change** -  The oEmbed Endpoint in KMS is now able to accept the entry page URL as input and not only the copied link from the 'share / oEmbed' tab. In addition to this type of URL: *https://[MediaSpace  URL]/id/[entry ID]?width=400&height=285&playerId=12345678*  this type of URL may be used: *https://[MediaSpace URL]/media/[Entry Name]/[Entry ID].* This improves the flexability with oEmbed-supported destinations. You can read more [here][2].

<p class="mce-heading-3">
  Resolved Issues
</p>

<table border="0">
  <thead>
    <tr>
      <td>
        <strong>ID#</strong>
      </td>
      
      <td>
        <strong>Summary</strong>
      </td>
    </tr>
  </thead>
  
  <tbody>
    <tr>
      <td>
        SUP-8954
      </td>
      
      <td style="text-align: left;">
        Upload CSS via KMS admin is now available in the Cssupload module. 
      </td>
    </tr>
    
    <tr>
      <td>
        SUP-8884 
      </td>
      
      <td style="text-align: left;">
        Image entries are no longer recognized as Audio entries in Analytics.
      </td>
    </tr>
    
    <tr>
      <td>
        SUP-9096
      </td>
      
      <td style="text-align: left;">
        The XSS vulnerability in KMS "404" page was fixed.
      </td>
    </tr>
